### üë• 3. PLC Scheduling & Tracking

#### 3.1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

**‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ doc_ref1.pdf ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ 11**:
- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î PLC Online **‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏∞ 1 ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á** ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏±‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î
- ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢: **500+ ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô** ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°
- ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢ "‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏µ‡πà-‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á"

#### 3.2 Database Schema (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

```prisma
// ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á PLCActivity ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà

model PLCGroup {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°
  groupName         String           @map("group_name")
  groupType         PLCGroupType     @map("group_type")
  province          String?          // ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö PROVINCIAL
  region            Region?          // ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö REGIONAL
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  facilitatorId     String?          @map("facilitator_id") // user_id
  facilitatorName   String?          @map("facilitator_name")
  description       String?          @db.Text
  
  // ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å
  members           PLCMember[]
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°
  sessions          PLCSession[]
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("plc_group")
}

enum PLCGroupType {
  PROVINCIAL        // ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏±‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î
  REGIONAL          // ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏†‡∏π‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏Ñ
  NATIONAL          // ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏®
  SUBJECT_BASED     // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ä‡∏≤
  COHORT_BASED      // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô
}

model PLCMember {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  groupId           String           @map("group_id")
  teacherId         String           @map("teacher_id")
  
  role              PLCRole          @default(PARTICIPANT)
  joinedAt          DateTime         @default(now()) @map("joined_at")
  isActive          Boolean          @default(true) @map("is_active")
  
  group             PLCGroup         @relation(fields: [groupId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  teacher           Teacher          @relation(fields: [teacherId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@unique([groupId, teacherId])
  @@map("plc_member")
}

model PLCSession {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  groupId           String           @map("group_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î
  sessionDate       DateTime         @map("session_date")
  sessionTime       String           @map("session_time") // "14:00-16:00"
  platform          String           // Zoom, Google Meet, Onsite
  meetingLink       String?          @map("meeting_link")
  location          String?          // ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Onsite
  
  // ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠
  topic             String
  description       String?          @db.Text
  agenda            String?          @db.Text
  
  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  facilitatorId     String?          @map("facilitator_id")
  facilitatorName   String           @map("facilitator_name")
  presenters        PLCPresenter[]
  
  // Status
  status            PLCSessionStatus @default(SCHEDULED)
  
  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°
  participants      PLCParticipant[]
  
  // ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£
  materials         PLCMaterial[]
  
  // ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏ú‡∏•
  summary           String?          @db.Text
  keyTakeaways      String?          @map("key_takeaways") @db.Text
  actionItems       String?          @map("action_items") @db.Text
  nextSessionDate   DateTime?        @map("next_session_date")
  
  group             PLCGroup         @relation(fields: [groupId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("plc_session")
}

enum PLCSessionStatus {
  SCHEDULED         // ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  ONGOING           // ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  COMPLETED         // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏™‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô
  CANCELLED         // ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å
}

model PLCPresenter {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  sessionId         String           @map("session_id")
  teacherId         String           @map("teacher_id")
  
  presentationTitle String           @map("presentation_title")
  presentationTime  String?          @map("presentation_time") // "14:30-15:00"
  slidesUrl         String?          @map("slides_url")
  
  session           PLCSession       @relation(fields: [sessionId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  teacher           Teacher          @relation(fields: [teacherId], references: [id])
  
  @@map("plc_presenter")
}

model PLCParticipant {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  sessionId         String           @map("session_id")
  teacherId         String           @map("teacher_id")
  
  registeredAt      DateTime         @default(now()) @map("registered_at")
  attended          Boolean          @default(false)
  checkInTime       DateTime?        @map("check_in_time")
  checkOutTime      DateTime?       @map("check_out_time")
  
  // Feedback
  feedback          String?          @db.Text
  rating            Int?             // 1-5
  takeaway          String?          @db.Text
  
  session           PLCSession       @relation(fields: [sessionId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  teacher           Teacher          @relation(fields: [teacherId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@unique([sessionId, teacherId])
  @@map("plc_participant")
}

model PLCMaterial {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  sessionId         String           @map("session_id")
  
  title             String
  fileUrl           String           @map("file_url")
  fileType          String           @map("file_type")
  uploadedAt        DateTime         @default(now()) @map("uploaded_at")
  
  session           PLCSession       @relation(fields: [sessionId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@map("plc_material")
}
```

#### 3.3 API Endpoints (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

**File**: `apps/api/src/plc/plc-scheduling.controller.ts`

```typescript
@Controller('plc')
export class PLCSchedulingController {
  
  // ===== Group Management =====
  
  @Get('groups')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° PLC' })
  async getGroups(@Query() query: {
    groupType?: PLCGroupType;
    province?: string;
    region?: Region;
  }) {
    // Return: groups + member count
  }
  
  @Post('groups')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° PLC' })
  async createGroup(@Body() dto: CreatePLCGroupDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á group
  }
  
  @Post('groups/:id/members')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°' })
  async addMember(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: { teacherId: string; role?: PLCRole }
  ) {
    // ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° member
  }
  
  // ===== Session Management =====
  
  @Get('sessions')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ PLC Sessions' })
  async getSessions(@Query() query: {
    groupId?: string;
    teacherId?: string;
    status?: PLCSessionStatus;
    startDate?: string;
    endDate?: string;
  }) {
    // Return: sessions
  }
  
  @Post('sessions')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á PLC Session' })
  async createSession(@Body() dto: CreatePLCSessionDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á session
    // Auto-invite group members
  }
  
  @Post('sessions/:id/schedule-next')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ' })
  async scheduleNext(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: { nextDate: string; nextTime: string }
  ) {
    // ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î nextSessionDate
  }
  
  // ===== Attendance =====
  
  @Post('sessions/:id/register')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°' })
  async register(@Param('id') id: string, @Body() dto: { teacherId: string }) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á PLCParticipant
  }
  
  @Post('sessions/:id/attendance')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°' })
  async recordAttendance(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: { participantIds: string[]; checkInTime?: string }
  ) {
    // Update attended = true
  }
  
  @Get('sessions/:id/attendance')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°' })
  async getAttendance(@Param('id') id: string) {
    // Return: {
    //   total: 50,
    //   attended: 45,
    //   absent: 5,
    //   attendanceRate: 90%
    // }
  }
  
  // ===== Tracking =====
  
  @Get('tracking/participation')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°' })
  async getParticipationTracking(@Query() query: {
    teacherId?: string;
    groupId?: string;
    startDate?: string;
    endDate?: string;
  }) {
    // Return: {
    //   teacherId: "xxx",
    //   totalSessions: 12,
    //   attended: 10,
    //   attendanceRate: 83.3%,
    //   missedSessions: [...]
    // }
  }
  
  @Get('tracking/stats')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏° PLC' })
  async getStats(@Query() query: {
    groupId?: string;
    period?: string;
  }) {
    // Return: {
    //   totalSessions: 50,
    //   totalParticipants: 500,
    //   averageAttendanceRate: 85%,
    //   activeGroups: 44
    // }
  }
}
```

### üí≠ 4. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏û‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏á (Mentor-Reflection System)

#### 4.1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

**‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ doc_ref1.pdf ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ 4**:
- ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö online (Reflective Portfolio)
- ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ (Learning Journal) **‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô**
- ‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏û‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£

#### 4.2 Database Schema (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

```prisma
// ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á ReflectiveJournal ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà

model JournalComment {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  journalId         String           @map("journal_id")
  
  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô
  commenterId       String           @map("commenter_id") // user_id
  commenterName     String           @map("commenter_name")
  commenterRole     String           @map("commenter_role") // MENTOR, PRINCIPAL
  
  // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô
  comment           String           @db.Text
  isPrivate         Boolean          @default(false) @map("is_private") // ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö
  parentCommentId   String?          @map("parent_comment_id")
  parentComment     JournalComment?  @relation("CommentReplies", fields: [parentCommentId], references: [id])
  replies           JournalComment[] @relation("CommentReplies")
  
  journal           ReflectiveJournal @relation(fields: [journalId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("journal_comment")
}

model ReflectionDiscussion {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  journalId         String           @map("journal_id")
  
  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤
  initiatorId       String           @map("initiator_id") // user_id
  initiatorRole     String           @map("initiator_role")
  
  // ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤
  topic             String
  discussionPoints  String           @map("discussion_points") @db.Text
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤
  messages          DiscussionMessage[]
  
  // Status
  status            DiscussionStatus @default(OPEN)
  resolvedAt        DateTime?        @map("resolved_at")
  
  journal           ReflectiveJournal @relation(fields: [journalId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("reflection_discussion")
}

enum DiscussionStatus {
  OPEN
  IN_PROGRESS
  RESOLVED
  CLOSED
}

model DiscussionMessage {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  discussionId     String           @map("discussion_id")
  
  senderId          String           @map("sender_id") // user_id
  senderName        String           @map("sender_name")
  senderRole        String           @map("sender_role")
  
  message           String           @db.Text
  attachments       Json?            // Array of file URLs
  
  discussion        ReflectionDiscussion @relation(fields: [discussionId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  
  @@map("discussion_message")
}

// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° relation ‡πÉ‡∏ô ReflectiveJournal
// comments        JournalComment[]
// discussions     ReflectionDiscussion[]
```

#### 4.3 API Endpoints (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

**File**: `apps/api/src/journal/journal-reflection.controller.ts`

```typescript
@Controller('journal')
export class JournalReflectionController {
  
  // ===== Comments =====
  
  @Post(':id/comments')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô Journal' })
  async addComment(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: CreateJournalCommentDto
  ) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á comment
    // ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á Notification ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π
  }
  
  @Get(':id/comments')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î' })
  async getComments(@Param('id') id: string) {
    // Return: comments (nested replies)
  }
  
  @Put('comments/:commentId')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô' })
  async updateComment(
    @Param('commentId') commentId: string,
    @Body() dto: UpdateJournalCommentDto
  ) {
    // ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç comment
  }
  
  // ===== Discussions =====
  
  @Post(':id/discussions')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤' })
  async createDiscussion(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: CreateDiscussionDto
  ) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á discussion
  }
  
  @Post('discussions/:id/messages')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤' })
  async sendMessage(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: CreateMessageDto
  ) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á message
    // ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á Notification
  }
  
  @Get('discussions/:id/messages')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î' })
  async getMessages(@Param('id') id: string) {
    // Return: messages (chronological)
  }
  
  @Post('discussions/:id/resolve')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤ (‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)' })
  async resolveDiscussion(@Param('id') id: string) {
    // Status: RESOLVED
  }
  
  // ===== Reflection Summary =====
  
  @Get('teacher/:teacherId/reflection-summary')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î' })
  async getReflectionSummary(@Param('teacherId') teacherId: string) {
    // Return: {
    //   totalJournals: 12,
    //   totalComments: 45,
    //   activeDiscussions: 3,
    //   mentorEngagement: 85%,
    //   ...
    // }
  }
}
```

```
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
```

---

### üëî 5. Role ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£ = Development Leader

#### 5.1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

**‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ doc_ref1.pdf ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ 5**:
- ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó **"‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤"** (Development Leader)
- ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å(‡∏©‡πå)‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡πà‡∏ô
- ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°-‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô-‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏µ

#### 5.2 Database Schema (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

```prisma
// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô User model ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà

model DevelopmentLeader {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  userId            String           @unique @map("user_id")
  schoolId          String?          @map("school_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£
  fullName          String           @map("full_name")
  position          String           // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£, ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  email             String           @unique
  phone             String?
  
  // ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•
  teachers          Teacher[]        // Relation through school
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤
  developmentActivities DevelopmentActivity[]
  
  // Dashboard Access
  dashboardAccess   Json?            @map("dashboard_access") // Permissions
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  user              User             @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id])
  school            School?          @relation(fields: [schoolId], references: [id])
  
  @@map("development_leader")
}

model DevelopmentActivity {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  leaderId          String           @map("leader_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°
  activityType      DevelopmentActivityType @map("activity_type")
  activityDate      DateTime         @map("activity_date")
  title             String
  description       String?          @db.Text
  
  // ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
  teachersInvolved  Json?            @map("teachers_involved") // Array of teacher IDs
  
  // ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå
  outcomes          String?          @db.Text
  impact            String?          @db.Text
  
  leader            DevelopmentLeader @relation(fields: [leaderId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  
  @@map("development_activity")
}

enum DevelopmentActivityType {
  ORIENTATION       // ‡∏õ‡∏ê‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏®
  WORKSHOP          // ‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏°
  MEETING           // ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏°
  SITE_VISIT        // ‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô
  MENTORING         // ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏®
  SUPPORT           // ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô
  EVALUATION        // ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô
  PLANNING          // ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô
}

model SchoolDevelopmentPlan {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  schoolId          String           @map("school_id")
  leaderId          String           @map("leader_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô
  year              Int
  planName          String           @map("plan_name")
  objectives        String           @db.Text
  strategies        String           @db.Text
  activities        String           @db.Text
  
  // Timeline
  startDate         DateTime         @map("start_date")
  endDate           DateTime         @map("end_date")
  
  // Status
  status            PlanStatus       @default(DRAFT)
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°
  progressReviews   SchoolPlanReview[]
  
  school            School           @relation(fields: [schoolId], references: [id])
  leader            DevelopmentLeader @relation(fields: [leaderId], references: [id])
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("school_development_plan")
}

model SchoolPlanReview {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  planId            String           @map("plan_id")
  
  reviewDate        DateTime         @map("review_date")
  reviewPeriod      String           @map("review_period") // Q1, Q2, Q3, Q4, Annual
  progress          String           @db.Text
  achievements      String?          @db.Text
  challenges        String?          @db.Text
  adjustments       String?          @db.Text
  
  plan              SchoolDevelopmentPlan @relation(fields: [planId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@map("school_plan_review")
}
```

#### 5.3 API Endpoints (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

```typescript
@Controller('development-leader')
export class DevelopmentLeaderController {
  
  @Get('dashboard')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: 'Dashboard ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£' })
  async getDashboard(@Request() req) {
    // Return: {
    //   schoolInfo: {...},
    //   teachersCount: 5,

    //   plcParticipationRate: 85%,
    //   upcomingActivities: [...],
    //   alerts: [...]
    // }
  }
  
  @Get('teachers')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•' })
  async getTeachers(@Request() req) {
    // Return: teachers in school
  }
  
  @Get('teachers/:teacherId/summary')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π' })
  async getTeacherSummary(@Param('teacherId') teacherId: string) {
    // Return: {
    //   idpProgress: {...},
    //   assessmentHistory: [...],
    //   siteVisits: [...],
    //   plcParticipation: [...],
    //   riskLevel: "LOW"
    // }
  }
  
  @Post('activities')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤' })
  async createActivity(@Body() dto: CreateDevelopmentActivityDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á activity
  }
  
  @Get('activities')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤' })
  async getActivities(@Query() query: {
    startDate?: string;
    endDate?: string;
    activityType?: DevelopmentActivityType;
  }) {
    // Return: activities
  }
  
  @Post('school-plan')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏£‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô' })
  async createSchoolPlan(@Body() dto: CreateSchoolDevelopmentPlanDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á plan
  }
  
  @Get('school-plan')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏£‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô' })
  async getSchoolPlan(@Query('year') year: number) {
    // Return: plan + reviews
  }
  
  @Post('school-plan/:id/review')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤' })
  async reviewPlan(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: CreatePlanReviewDto
  ) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á review
  }
  
  @Get('reports/summary')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤' })
  async getSummaryReport(@Query() query: {
    period?: string;

  }
```

```
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ ‚ö†Ô∏è ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°                    ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  Upcoming Activities:                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ üìÖ 20 ‡∏°.‡∏Ñ. - Site Visit (‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏Å) ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ üìÖ 25 ‡∏°.‡∏Ñ. - PLC Session        ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò   ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  [üìù ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°] [üìä ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô] [‚öôÔ∏è ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤] ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

---

## üìä ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°: ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°

### üè∑Ô∏è 1. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π (Teacher Segmentation)

#### 1.1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

**‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ doc_ref1.pdf ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ 5**:
- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö **Personalized**
- ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≥ **65 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô** ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠
- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°: ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏î, ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà, ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á, ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à

#### 1.2 Database Schema (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

```prisma
// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô schema.prisma

model TeacherTag {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  name              String           @unique
  description       String?          @db.Text
  category          TagCategory
  color             String?          // ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏• UI (#FF5733)
  icon              String?          // Icon name
  
  teachers          TeacherTagRelation[]
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("teacher_tag")
}

enum TagCategory {
  SKILL             // ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏© (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏µ, ‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ô Active Learning)
  INTEREST          // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô STEM, ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢, ‡∏®‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏õ‡∏∞)
  RISK              // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà, ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤)
  ROLE              // ‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó (‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≥, ‡∏û‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏á, ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á)
  NEED              // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤ (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ä‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô)
  ACHIEVEMENT       // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏î‡πà‡∏ô, ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏•)
  COHORT            // ‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô (‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô 1, ‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô 2)
}

model TeacherTagRelation {
  teacherId         String           @map("teacher_id")
  tagId             String           @map("tag_id")
  addedAt           DateTime         @default(now()) @map("added_at")
  addedBy           String?          @map("added_by") // user_id
  notes             String?          @db.Text // ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏
  
  teacher           Teacher          @relation(fields: [teacherId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  tag               TeacherTag       @relation(fields: [tagId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@id([teacherId, tagId])
  @@map("teacher_tag_relation")
}

model TeacherSegment {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°
  segmentName       String           @map("segment_name")
  segmentType       SegmentType      @map("segment_type")
  description       String?          @db.Text
  criteria          Json             // ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° (JSON)
  
  // ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å
  members           TeacherSegmentMember[]
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤
  developmentFocus  String?          @map("development_focus") @db.Text
  targetOutcomes    String?          @map("target_outcomes") @db.Text
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("teacher_segment")
}

enum SegmentType {
  BY_SKILL          // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏∞
  BY_INTEREST       // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à
  BY_RISK           // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á
  BY_ROLE           // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó
  BY_AREA           // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà
  BY_SUBJECT        // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ä‡∏≤
  BY_COHORT         // ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô
  CUSTOM            // ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
}

model TeacherSegmentMember {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  segmentId         String           @map("segment_id")
  teacherId         String           @map("teacher_id")
  
  joinedAt          DateTime         @default(now()) @map("joined_at")
  joinedBy          String?          @map("joined_by") // user_id
  notes             String?          @db.Text
  
  segment           TeacherSegment   @relation(fields: [segmentId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  teacher           Teacher          @relation(fields: [teacherId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@unique([segmentId, teacherId])
  @@map("teacher_segment_member")
}

// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° field ‡πÉ‡∏ô Teacher model
// isCoreTeam        Boolean          @default(false) @map("is_core_team") // ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≥ 65 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô
// tags              TeacherTagRelation[]
// segments          TeacherSegmentMember[]
```

```typescript
@Controller('teachers/segmentation')
export class SegmentationController {
  
  // ===== Tags =====
  
  @Get('tags')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Tags ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î' })
  async getTags(@Query() query: {
    category?: TagCategory;
    search?: string;
  }) {
    // Return: tags
  }
  
  @Post('tags')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Tag ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà' })
  async createTag(@Body() dto: CreateTagDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á tag
  }
  
  @Post('teachers/:teacherId/tags')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Tag ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π' })
  async addTagToTeacher(
    @Param('teacherId') teacherId: string,
    @Body() dto: { tagId: string; notes?: string }
  ) {
    // ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° tag relation
  }
  
  @Delete('teachers/:teacherId/tags/:tagId')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏•‡∏ö Tag ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π' })
  async removeTagFromTeacher(
    @Param('teacherId') teacherId: string,
    @Param('tagId') tagId: string
  ) {
    // ‡∏•‡∏ö tag relation
  }
  
  // ===== Segments =====
  
  @Get('segments')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Segments' })
  async getSegments(@Query() query: {
    segmentType?: SegmentType;
    search?: string;
  }) {
    // Return: segments + member count
  }
  
  @Post('segments')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Segment ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà' })
  async createSegment(@Body() dto: CreateSegmentDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á segment
  }
  
  @Post('segments/:id/members')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô Segment' })
  async addMember(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: { teacherIds: string[] }
  ) {
    // ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° members
  }
  
  @Get('segments/:id/members')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å' })
  async getMembers(@Param('id') id: string) {
    // Return: members + teacher details
  }
  
  // ===== Auto Segmentation =====
  
  @Post('auto-segment')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥' })
  async autoSegment(@Body() dto: {
    segmentType: SegmentType;
    criteria: any; // JSON criteria
  }) {
    // ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå
    // Return: { segmentId, members: [...] }
  }
  
  // ===== Core Team =====
  
  @Get('core-team')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≥ (65 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô)' })
  async getCoreTeam(@Query() query: {
    region?: string;
    province?: string;
  }) {
    // Return: teachers where isCoreTeam = true
  }
  
  @Post('teachers/:teacherId/core-team')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≥' })
  async setCoreTeam(
    @Param('teacherId') teacherId: string,
    @Body() dto: { isCoreTeam: boolean }
  ) {
    // Update isCoreTeam flag
  }
  
  // ===== Analytics =====
  
  @Get('analytics/overview')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°' })
  async getAnalytics() {
    // Return: {
    //   totalSegments: 20,
    //   totalTags: 50,
    //   coreTeamCount: 65,
    //   segmentDistribution: {...},
    //   tagUsage: {...}
    // }
```

---

### ‚ö†Ô∏è 2. Risk Assessment (‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á)

#### 2.1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

**‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ doc_ref1.pdf ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ 5-6**:
- ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©
- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Personalized
- ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ

#### 2.2 Database Schema (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

```prisma
// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô schema.prisma

model TeacherRiskAssessment {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  teacherId         String           @map("teacher_id")
  assessmentDate    DateTime         @map("assessment_date")
  assessorId        String           @map("assessor_id") // user_id
  assessorName      String           @map("assessor_name")
  
  // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á 4 ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥
  personalRisk      RiskLevel        @map("personal_risk")
  personalFactors   String?          @map("personal_factors") @db.Text
  emotionalRisk     RiskLevel        @map("emotional_risk")
  emotionalFactors  String?          @map("emotional_factors") @db.Text
  socialRisk        RiskLevel        @map("social_risk")
  socialFactors     String?          @map("social_factors") @db.Text
  professionalRisk  RiskLevel        @map("professional_risk")
  professionalFactors String?         @map("professional_factors") @db.Text
  
  // ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°
  overallRisk       RiskLevel        @map("overall_risk")
  riskScore         Int              @map("risk_score") // 1-20 (‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° 4 ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥)
  riskFactors       String           @map("risk_factors") @db.Text
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°
  indicators        Json?            // Array of risk indicators
  evidence          String?          @db.Text
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞
  recommendations   String           @db.Text
  supportNeeded     String?          @map("support_needed") @db.Text
  priority          PriorityLevel    @default(MEDIUM)
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°
  followUpRequired  Boolean          @default(false) @map("follow_up_required")
  followUpDate      DateTime?        @map("follow_up_date")
  followUpNotes     String?          @map("follow_up_notes") @db.Text
  
  teacher           Teacher          @relation(fields: [teacherId], references: [id])
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("teacher_risk_assessment")
}

enum RiskLevel {
  LOW               // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥ (1-5)
  MEDIUM            // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á (6-10)
  HIGH              // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á (11-15)
  CRITICAL          // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏§‡∏ï (16-20)
}

enum PriorityLevel {
  LOW
  MEDIUM
  HIGH
  URGENT
}

model SpecialSupport {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  teacherId         String           @map("teacher_id")
  riskAssessmentId String?          @map("risk_assessment_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô
  supportType       SupportType
  supportCategory   String           @map("support_category") // ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏à‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏≤, ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£, ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏°
  description       String           @db.Text
  reason            String           @db.Text
  
  // Timeline
  startDate         DateTime         @map("start_date")
  endDate           DateTime?        @map("end_date")
  expectedOutcome   String?          @map("expected_outcome") @db.Text
  
  // Status
  status            SupportStatus    @default(ACTIVE)
  
  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ä‡∏≠‡∏ö
  assignedTo        String?          @map("assigned_to") // user_id
  assignedToName     String?          @map("assigned_to_name")
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°
  progress          String?          @db.Text
  outcomes           String?          @db.Text
  effectiveness     Int?             // 1-5
  
  teacher           Teacher          @relation(fields: [teacherId], references: [id])
  riskAssessment   TeacherRiskAssessment? @relation(fields: [riskAssessmentId], references: [id])
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("special_support")
}

enum SupportStatus {
  PLANNED           // ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  ACTIVE            // ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  COMPLETED         // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏™‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô
  CANCELLED         // ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å
}

model RiskIndicator {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  
  indicatorCode     String           @unique @map("indicator_code") // ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô RISK_001
  indicatorName     String           @map("indicator_name")
  category          RiskCategory
  description       String?          @db.Text
  weight            Int              @default(1) // ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å 1-5
  
  @@map("risk_indicator")
}

enum RiskCategory {
  ATTENDANCE        // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°
  PERFORMANCE       // ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
  RELATIONSHIP      // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå
  STRESS            // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
  ADAPTATION        // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß
  OTHER             // ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ
}
```

#### 2.3 API Endpoints (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

**File**: `apps/api/src/risk/risk-assessment.controller.ts`

```typescript
@Controller('risk-assessment')
export class RiskAssessmentController {
  
  @Post()
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á' })
  async create(@Body() dto: CreateRiskAssessmentDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á assessment
    // ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì overallRisk ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ riskScore
    // ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ HIGH ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ CRITICAL ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á SpecialSupport ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
  }
  
  @Get('teacher/:teacherId')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á' })
  async getByTeacher(@Param('teacherId') teacherId: string) {
    // Return: array of assessments (sorted by date)
  }
  
  @Get('teacher/:teacherId/current')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô' })
  async getCurrent(@Param('teacherId') teacherId: string) {
    // Return: latest assessment
  }
  
  @Get('high-risk')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á' })
  async getHighRisk(@Query() query: {
    riskLevel?: RiskLevel;
    region?: string;
    province?: string;
    priority?: PriorityLevel;
  }) {
    // Return: teachers with HIGH or CRITICAL risk
  }
  
  @Get('dashboard')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: 'Dashboard ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á' })
  async getDashboard(@Query() query: {
    region?: string;
    province?: string;
  }) {
    // Return: {
    //   totalTeachers: 327,
    //   lowRisk: 250,
    //   mediumRisk: 50,
    //   highRisk: 20,
    //   criticalRisk: 7,
    //   riskDistribution: {...},
    //   urgentActions: [...]
    // }
  }
  
  @Get('stats')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á' })
  async getStats() {
    // Return: ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°
  }
  
  // ===== Special Support =====
  
  @Post('special-support')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©' })
  async createSupport(@Body() dto: CreateSpecialSupportDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á support plan
  }
  
  @Get('special-support')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©' })
  async getSupports(@Query() query: {
    teacherId?: string;
    status?: SupportStatus;
    supportType?: SupportType;
  }) {
    // Return: supports
  }
  
  @Put('special-support/:id')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô' })
  async updateSupport(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: UpdateSpecialSupportDto
  ) {
    // ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï support
  }
  
  @Post('special-support/:id/complete')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô' })
  async completeSupport(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: { outcomes: string; effectiveness: number }
  ) {
    // Status: COMPLETED
  }
}
```

```
‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò   ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  High Risk Teachers:                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê   ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  ‚îÇ - Emotional: CRITICAL           ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ - Social: MEDIUM                ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ - Professional: HIGH            ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ                                 ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ ‚ö†Ô∏è ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏£‡πà‡∏á‡∏î‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô              ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ [‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î] [‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠] ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  Risk Trend:                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ Line Chart: ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤    ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îÇ [‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏°]                    ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò   ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

### üí∞ 3. Budget Tracking (‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì 3.78 ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó)

#### 3.1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

**‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ doc_ref1.pdf ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ 17-22**:
- **‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°**: 3,780,000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó
- **‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì**:
  - ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: 100,000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó
  - Workshop & Training: 1,354,050 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó
  - Site Visit: 1,637,950 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó
  - ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ: 40,000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó
  - ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£: 648,000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó

#### 3.2 Database Schema (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

```prisma
// ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô schema.prisma

model ProjectBudget {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì
  year              Int              // ‡∏õ‡∏µ‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì (2568)
  budgetName        String           @map("budget_name") // "‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å(‡∏©‡πå)‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡πà‡∏ô 2568"
  totalAllocated    Decimal          @map("total_allocated") @db.Decimal(12, 2) // 3,780,000
  totalSpent        Decimal          @default(0) @map("total_spent") @db.Decimal(12, 2)
  totalRemaining    Decimal          @map("total_remaining") @db.Decimal(12, 2)
  
  // ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì
  categories        BudgetCategory[]
  
  // Status
  status            BudgetStatus     @default(ACTIVE)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@unique([year])
  @@map("project_budget")
}

enum BudgetStatus {
  DRAFT             // ‡∏£‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
  ACTIVE            // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
  CLOSED            // ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
}

model BudgetCategory {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  budgetId          String           @map("budget_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î
  category          BudgetCategoryType
  categoryName      String           @map("category_name")
  allocated         Decimal          @db.Decimal(12, 2)
  spent             Decimal          @default(0) @db.Decimal(12, 2)
  remaining         Decimal          @db.Decimal(12, 2)
  
  // ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ã‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå
  allocationPercent Float            @map("allocation_percent") // % ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°
  spentPercent      Float            @default(0) @map("spent_percent") // % ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  
  // Expenses
  expenses          BudgetExpense[]
  
  budget            ProjectBudget    @relation(fields: [budgetId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  @@map("budget_category")
}

enum BudgetCategoryType {
  DATABASE          // ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (100,000)
  TRAINING          // ‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏° (1,354,050)
  SITE_VISIT        // ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà (1,637,950)
  AUDIT             // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö (40,000)
  PERSONNEL         // ‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£ (648,000)
  MATERIAL          // ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏™‡∏î‡∏∏
  EQUIPMENT         // ‡∏≠‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå
  TRANSPORTATION    // ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
  ACCOMMODATION     // ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏±‡∏Å
  MEALS             // ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£
  OTHER             // ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ
}

model BudgetExpense {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  categoryId        String           @map("category_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
  expenseDate       DateTime         @map("expense_date")
  description       String           @db.Text
  amount            Decimal          @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  
  // ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
  vendor            String?          // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏¢/‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  invoiceNumber     String?          @map("invoice_number")
  paymentMethod     PaymentMethod    @map("payment_method")
  
  // ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£
  receiptUrl        String?          @map("receipt_url")
  invoiceUrl        String?          @map("invoice_url")
  attachments       Json?            // Array of file URLs
  
  // ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
  status            ExpenseStatus    @default(PENDING)
  requestedBy       String           @map("requested_by") // user_id
  requestedByName   String           @map("requested_by_name")
  approvedBy        String?          @map("approved_by")
  approvedByName    String?          @map("approved_by_name")
  approvedAt        DateTime?        @map("approved_at")
  rejectionReason   String?          @map("rejection_reason") @db.Text
  
  // Metadata
  notes             String?          @db.Text
  
  category          BudgetCategory   @relation(fields: [categoryId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt         DateTime         @updatedAt @map("updated_at")
  
  @@map("budget_expense")
}

enum PaymentMethod {
  CASH              // ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏î
  TRANSFER          // ‡πÇ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô
  CHECK             // ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πá‡∏Ñ
  CREDIT_CARD       // ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏ï
  OTHER             // ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ
}

enum ExpenseStatus {
  PENDING           // ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
  APPROVED          // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  REJECTED          // ‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò
  PAID              // ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  CANCELLED         // ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å
}

model BudgetAlert {
  id                String           @id @default(uuid())
  categoryId        String           @map("category_id")
  
  // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• Alert
  alertType         AlertType        @map("alert_type")
  message           String           @db.Text
  threshold         Decimal?         @db.Decimal(10, 2) // ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô
  
  // Status
  isRead            Boolean          @default(false) @map("is_read")
  readBy            String?          @map("read_by")
  readAt            DateTime?        @map("read_at")
  
  category          BudgetCategory   @relation(fields: [categoryId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  
  createdAt         DateTime         @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  
  @@map("budget_alert")
}

enum AlertType {
  APPROACHING_LIMIT // ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏á‡∏ö
  EXCEEDED          // ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏á‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  LOW_BALANCE       // ‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢
  UNUSUAL_EXPENSE   // ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥
}
```

#### 3.3 API Endpoints (‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î)

**File**: `apps/api/src/budget/budget.controller.ts`

```typescript
@Controller('budget')
export class BudgetController {
  
  // ===== Budget Management =====
  
  @Get()
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î' })
  async getBudgets(@Query() query: { year?: number }) {
    // Return: budgets
  }
  
  @Get(':year')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏µ' })
  async getBudgetByYear(@Param('year') year: number) {
    // Return: budget + categories + summary
  }
  
  @Post()
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà' })
  async createBudget(@Body() dto: CreateBudgetDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á budget + categories
  }
  
  // ===== Categories =====
  
  @Get(':year/categories')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì' })
  async getCategories(@Param('year') year: number) {
    // Return: categories with spent/remaining
  }
  
  @Get(':year/category/:categoryType')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏î‡∏π‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î' })
  async getCategory(
    @Param('year') year: number,
    @Param('categoryType') categoryType: BudgetCategoryType
  ) {
    // Return: category + expenses
  }
  
  // ===== Expenses =====
  
  @Post('expenses')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢' })
  async createExpense(@Body() dto: CreateExpenseDto) {
    // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á expense (Status: PENDING)
    // Update category.spent, remaining
    // Check alerts
  }
  
  @Get('expenses')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢' })
  async getExpenses(@Query() query: {
    categoryId?: string;
    status?: ExpenseStatus;
    startDate?: string;
    endDate?: string;
    page?: number;
    limit?: number;
  }) {
    // Return: expenses + pagination
  }
  
  @Put('expenses/:id/approve')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢' })
  async approveExpense(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: { approvedBy: string }
  ) {
    // Status: APPROVED
    // Update category.spent
  }
  
  @Put('expenses/:id/reject')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢' })
  async rejectExpense(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Body() dto: { rejectedBy: string; reason: string }
  ) {
    // Status: REJECTED
  }
  
  @Put('expenses/:id/mark-paid')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß' })
  async markPaid(@Param('id') id: string) {
    // Status: PAID
  }
  
  // ===== Dashboard & Reports =====
  
  @Get('dashboard/:year')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: 'Dashboard ‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì' })
  async getDashboard(@Param('year') year: number) {
    // Return: {
    //   totalAllocated: 3,780,000,
    //   totalSpent: 2,500,000,
    //   totalRemaining: 1,280,000,
    //   spentPercent: 66.1%,
    //   categories: [...],
    //   alerts: [...],
    //   recentExpenses: [...]
    // }
  }
  
  @Get('reports/:year/summary')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì' })
  async getSummaryReport(
    @Param('year') year: number,
    @Query() query: { format?: 'pdf' | 'excel' }
  ) {
    // Return: report
  }
  
  @Get('reports/:year/detailed')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î' })
  async getDetailedReport(
    @Param('year') year: number,
    @Query() query: {
      categoryType?: BudgetCategoryType;
      startDate?: string;
      endDate?: string;
    }
  ) {
    // Return: detailed report
  }
  
  // ===== Alerts =====
  
  @Get('alerts')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Alert' })
  async getAlerts(@Query() query: {
    categoryId?: string;
    isRead?: boolean;
  }) {
    // Return: alerts
  }
  
  @Put('alerts/:id/read')
  @ApiOperation({ summary: '‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Alert ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß' })
  async markAlertRead(@Param('id') id: string) {
    // isRead: true
  }
}
```

```
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§

‚îÇ  ‚îÇ üíµ ‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠: 1,280,000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó       ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ
```

#### 3.5 Workflow & Business Logic

**Workflow ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì**:

```
   ‚Üì
```

**Business Rules**:
- ‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° = 3,780,000 ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó (‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£)

- ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 100% ‚Üí Alert + Block ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
